import optuna
optuna.logging.disable_default_handler()

def add_study(fn, name, sampler=None, n_trials=200):
    study = optuna.create_study(
        direction="minimize",
        storage="sqlite:///db.sqlite3",
        study_name=name,
        sampler=sampler
    )
    study.optimize(fn, n_trials=n_trials, show_progress_bar=True)
    print(f"Best value: {study.best_value} (params: {study.best_params})")

 def example1(trial):
    x = trial.suggest_float("x", -100, 100)
    y = trial.suggest_float("y", -100, 100)
    return x**2 + y**2


add_study(example1, "Test 1") # OK

def example1_another_sampler_random(trial):
    x = trial.suggest_float("x", -100, 100)
    y = trial.suggest_float("y", -100, 100)
    return x**2 + y**2

add_study(example1_another_sampler_random, "Test 1 (Random Sampler)", sampler=optuna.samplers.RandomSampler(), n_trials=500)

def example2(trial):
    x = trial.suggest_float("x", -100, 100)
    y = trial.suggest_float("y", -100, 100)
    return 1000 * (x - 10) ** 10 + 100 * (y + 20) ** 10

def example2_another_sampler_grid(trial):
    x = trial.suggest_float("x", -100, 100)
    y = trial.suggest_float("y", -100, 100)
    return 1000 * (x - 10) ** 10 + 100 * (y + 20) ** 10

search_space = {
    'x': [-10 + i for i in range(21)],
    'y': [-30 + i for i in range(21)]
}

n_trials = len(search_space['x']) * len(search_space['y'])

add_study(example2_another_sampler_grid, "Test 2 (Grid sampler)", sampler=optuna.samplers.GridSampler(search_space), n_trials=n_trials)

from numpy import cos, exp, pi
def example3(trial):
    x = trial.suggest_float("x", 100, 100)
    y = trial.suggest_float("y", 100, 100)
    return -cos(x) * cos(y) * exp(-((x - pi) ** 2 + (y - pi) ** 2))
add_study(example3, "Test 3") # no global minimum

from numpy import cos, sin
def example4(trial):
    x = trial.suggest_float("x", -100, 100)
    y = trial.suggest_float("y", -100, 100)
    return sin(3 / 5 * pi * x) ** 2 + (x / 5 - 1) ** 2 * (1 + sin(3 * pi * y / 5) ** 2) + (y / 5 - 1) ** 2 * (1 + sin(2 * pi * y / 5)**2)

add_study(example4, "Test 4")

import numpy as np
def example4_another_sampler_grid(trial):
    x = trial.suggest_float("x", -100, 100)
    y = trial.suggest_float("y", -100, 100)
    return sin(3 / 5 * pi * x) ** 2 + (x / 5 - 1) ** 2 * (1 + sin(3 * pi * y / 5) ** 2) + (y / 5 - 1) ** 2 * (1 + sin(2 * pi * y / 5)**2)

x_points = np.linspace(-10, 10, 21)
y_points = np.linspace(-10, 10, 21)

search_space = {
    'x': x_points.tolist(),
    'y': y_points.tolist()
}

n_trials = len(x_points) * len(y_points)

add_study(example4_another_sampler_grid, "Test 4 (Grid sampler)", sampler=optuna.samplers.GridSampler(search_space), n_trials=n_trials)

from numpy import arctan, pi

def example5(trial):
    x = trial.suggest_float("x", -100, 100)
    y = trial.suggest_float("y", -100, 100)
    return (arctan(x + 2 * y) - (pi / 2 - arctan(x - y))) ** 2

add_study(example5, "Test 5") # OK

import numpy as np 

def example6_with_another_sampler_grid(trial):
    x = trial.suggest_float("x", -100, 100)
    y = trial.suggest_float("y", -100, 100)
    return np.e**(np.float64((x+0.54719)**2)) + np.e**(np.float64((y+1.54719)**2))

x_points = np.linspace(-10, 10, 35)
y_points = np.linspace(-10, 10, 35)

search_space = {
    'x': x_points.tolist(),
    'y': y_points.tolist()
}

n_trials = len(x_points) * len(y_points)
add_study(example6_with_another_sampler_grid, "Test 6 (Grid sampler)", sampler=optuna.samplers.GridSampler(search_space), n_trials=n_trials)

import numpy as np
def example6_spec(trial):
    x = trial.suggest_float("x", -100, 100)
    y = trial.suggest_float("y", -100, 100)
    return np.e**(np.float64((x+0.54719)**2)) + np.e**(np.float64((y+1.54719)**2))

add_study(example6_spec, "Test 6 (CMA)", sampler=optuna.samplers.CmaEsSampler(), n_trials=500)
